LLM ANSWER

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
LLM ANSWER
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
It is not stated that Lapu-Lapu personally killed Magellan. Magellan was killed after losing a battle against the army of Lapulapu, chief of Mactan.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
LLM ANSWER
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Treaty of Paris (1898) stated that Spain ceded the Philippine Islands to the United States, with the U.S. occupying Manila until a peace treaty determined control over the Philippines.

LLM ANSWER
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
- Filipinos faced mass casualties during the occupation, with around 500,000 dying.  
- The Japanese conducted horrific human experiments on Filipinos, including amputations, dissections, and vivisections.  
- Infants were killed as an act of entertainment and stress relief by the Japanese.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
LLM ANSWER
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Katipunan (KKK) was founded on July 7, 1892 by Deodato Arellano, Andrés Bonifacio, Valentin Diaz, Ladislao Diwa, José Dizon, and Teodoro Plata with the purpose of achieving Filipino independence from Spain.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
LLM ANSWER
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Treaty of Paris (1898), which concluded the Spanish–American War, transferred the Philippines to the United States. This transition led to the Philippine-American War, as U.S. troops took control of the country, escalating into armed conflict. The treaty established the foundation for the subsequent war.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
LLM ANSWER
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Katipunan was a revolutionary organization leading the Philippine Revolution, which was the armed struggle against Spain. The Philippine Revolution refers to the actual war/revolution initiated by the Katipunan.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
LLM ANSWER
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
- Andrés C. Bonifacio was an unofficial president of the Sovereign Tagalog Nation and the Philippines (1896–1897).  
- He co-founded the Katipunan and served as its Supremo, reorganizing it into the Haring Bayang Katagalugan revolutionary government.  
- He is recognized as "The Father of the Philippine Revolution" and a national hero, though not officially listed in Philippine presidential records.  
- He was executed in Maragondon by Major Lázaro Macapagal under orders of the Consejo de la Guerra for sedition and treason.
